This script builds and installs the P4_16 (and also P4_14)
compiler, and the behavioral-model software packet forwarding
program, that can behave as just about any legal P4 program.

It regularly tested on freshly installed Ubuntu 16.04 and Ubuntu
18.04 systems, with all Ubuntu software updates as of the date
of testing.  See this directory for log files recording the last
date this script was tested on its supported operating systems:

    https://github.com/jafingerhut/p4-guide/tree/master/bin/output

The files installed by this script consume about 5 GB of disk space.

On a 2015 MacBook Pro with a decent speed Internet connection
and an SSD drive, running Ubuntu Linux in a VirtualBox VM, it
took about 40 minutes.

You will likely need to enter your password for multiple uses of
'sudo' spread throughout this script.

Versions of software that will be installed by this script:

+ protobuf: github.com/google/protobuf v3.2.0
+ behavioral-model: github.com/p4lang/behavioral-model latest version
  which, as of 2019-Jun-10, also installs these things:
  + thrift version 0.9.2
  + nanomsg version 1.0.0
  + nnpy git checkout c7e718a5173447c85182dc45f99e2abcf9cd4065 (latest as of 2015-Apr-22
+ p4c: github.com/p4lang/p4c latest version

Note that anything installed as 'the latest version' can change
its precise contents from one run of this script to another.
That is an intentional property of this script -- to get the
latest version of that software.  If you want particular
versions that are not the latest, you can modify this script by
adding 'git checkout <tag>' and/or 'git checkout <commit-sha>'
command at the appropriate places.

commit 33e221fd879c1aa2f16b04ab0adbf341619003ae
Author: Antonin Bas <abas@vmware.com>
Date:   Fri Sep 20 08:55:10 2019 -0700

    Cleanup the "parameters_vector" code
    
    This is the code that enables action primitives to take as parameters
    lists of values (for the moment, we are restricted to lists of Data
    objects).
    
    We refactor the code to get to a cleaner design: we no longer have a
    class (ActionParamVectorFn) that both inherits from and encapsulates
    another one (ActionFn). This led to less duplication and fewer lines of
    code.
    
    We have removed the check in P4Objects that verified that only arguments
    resolving to numerical values (i.e. that can be cast to Data) were added
    to vector of parameters. In theory we can support all homogeneous lists
    in bmv2, even though it is not the case yet. We should think of how we
    can define a proper check in the future: one that enforces that the list
    is homogeneous and the list type is supported by that version of bmv2.
    
    Some cleanup was done in the Gtests as well: we no longer use the
    console logger to verify that messages are logged properly, instead we
    use a string stream.
    
    The JSON version number was bumped up to 2.22, since it was not done in
    the original "parameters_vector" patch.

If you ever happen to want to link against installed libraries
in a given directory, LIBDIR, you must either use libtool, and
specify the full pathname of the library, or use the '-LLIBDIR'
